Angelic Buster Basics

Active Soul Buster
Master Level 1
Description Inherit Eskalade's power to control both the Soul Shooter and Soul Ring.
Level 1 MP Cost: 2, Hold the attack key to fire Eskalade's power forward
Can be used while moving. Max Enemies Hit: 3, Damage: 60%


Passive True Heart Inheritance
Master Level 1
Description Draw out Eskalade's true strength to enhance your Soul Shooter's hidden power.
Level 1 Soul Shooter Mastery: +10%


Active Grappling Heart
Master Level 1
Description Tosses a magical line above you to ascend to higher platforms.
Level 1 Move to the nearest platform above you.
Press jump while moving to cancel.
Show/hide all levels
Active Terms and Conditions
Master Level 3
Description Uses your mastery of contract law to temporarily boost Eskalade's damage.
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Duration: 10 sec, Damage: +60%
Effect reduced to half when used as a link skill
Cooldown: 90 sec
3 MP Cost: 30, Duration: 10 sec, Damage: +120%
Effect reduced to half when used as a link skill
Cooldown: 60 sec
Active Terms and Conditions
Master Level 3
Description Uses your mastery of contract law to temporarily boost Eskalade's damage.
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Duration: 10 sec, Damage: +60%
Effect reduced to half when used as a link skill

Active Day Dreamer
Master Level 1
Description Move to the Lovely Buster Suite.
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Return to the Lovely Buster Suite
Cooldown: 600 sec


Active Dress-Up
Master Level 1
Description Summon Eskalade's power to transform into Angelic Buster.
Level 1 MP Cost: 20, Transform into Angelic Buster
When used as Angelic Buster, transform back into Tear.


Active On Stage
Master Level 1
Description Hold an impromptu concert. Changes the background music of nearby characters to Angelic Buster concert music.
Level 1 MP Cost: 100, plays up to 5 tracks from Angelic Buster's album
Movement ends the concert, only usable in town
Cooldown: 1 hour


Active Exclusive Spell
Master Level 1
Description [Master Level: 1]
Increases the Attack Power and Magic ATT of all nearby characters.
Cooldown: 300 sec
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Attack Power and Magic ATT: +4%, Duration: 40 min

Master Level 10

Angelic Buster (III)

Show/hide all levels
Active Soul Seeker
Master Level 20
Description Compress the essence of Eskalade's power, then launch it at the enemy. The essence automatically tracks enemies, prioritizes the boss with the highest Max HP if within range, and is unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 10 required to learn Soul Seeker Expert.
Level 1 MP Cost: 13, Number of Essences: 2
Essence Damage: 206%, Number of Attacks: 1 until the max attack count is reached or it disappears
Chance for Essence to Respawn on Hit: 28%, Number of Attacks: 7
20 MP Cost: 19, Number of Essences: 2
Essence Damage: 320%, Number of Attacks: 1 until the max attack count is reached or it disappears
Chance for Essence to Respawn on Hit: 85%, Number of Attacks: 7

Active Soul Resonance
Master Level 30
Description Resonate with Eskalade's soul to draw out explosive energy. The energy draws enemies in and deals damage.
During the resonance, Eskalade prevents you from taking damage.
The invincibility ends when Soul Resonance ends. Enemy attacks cannot knock you back while the skill is being cast.
Level 1 MP Cost: 40, Invincibility Duration: 2 sec
Hold down the key to continuously attack up to 10 enemies, for 88% damage, 5 times.
Hold for at least 8 sec to make a final blow that deals up to 300% damage 5 times based on the time held. Boss Damage: +50%
While casting, any Max HP scaling damage taken is reduced by 35%.
Cooldown: 118 sec.
30 MP Cost: 40, Invincibility Duration: 2 sec

Active Erda Nova
Master Level 25
Description Collect Erda from within yourself and from the surrounding area, then detonate it around your enemies. The Erda of attacked enemies will become disrupted, which will bind their movements. Can deal damage to enemies even when they are under Attack Ignore. Also ignores Attack Reflection.
Level 1 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP, Damage: 156%, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Number of Attacks: 5, Bind Duration: 10 sec.
Bind Duration increases by up to 100% based on damage inflicted with Erda Nova.
Cooldown: 216 sec.

Active Erda Shower
Master Level 25
Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Level 1 HP Cost: 3000
Erdas Shower
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 6, Cooldown reduced by 2 sec per attacked enemy
Cooldown: 40 sec
Erda Fountain
Object Summon Duration: 60 sec. Every time enemies in a map with the summoned object are defeated, the Erda released from the enemies condenses around the object.
Defeating 12 or more will release the gathered Erda, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 4
Cooldown: 60 sec
Cooldown shared with Erdas Shower and Erda Fountain.

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec

Active Superstar Spotlight
Master Level 25
Description A real superstar brings their own spotlight everywhere they go. Enemies take damage under its rays because they are unworthy of the spotlight. Your own abilities are boosted while you bask in the glow. Unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 MP Cost: 600, Install 3 spotlights that shine on you for 30 sec
While you are within the spotlight, you gain Status Resistance +60, Critical Rate +30%, and Final Damage +9%.
Each spotlight deals 832% damage 3 times against up to 15 enemies within its area.
Each subsequent spotlight to hit the same enemy deals 75% less Final Damage.
Cooldown: 120 sec
25 MP Cost: 600, Install 3 spotlights that shine on you for 30 sec
While you are within the spotlight, you gain Status Resistance +75, Critical Rate +45%, and Final Damage +15%.
Each spotlight deals 1600% damage 3 times against up to 15 enemies within its area.
Each subsequent spotlight to hit the same enemy deals 75% less Final Damage.
Cooldown: 120 sec
30 MP Cost: 600, Install 3 spotlights that shine on you for 30 sec
While you are within the spotlight, you gain Status Resistance +78, Critical Rate +48%, and Final Damage +18%.
Each spotlight deals 1760% damage 3 times against up to 15 enemies within its area.
Each subsequent spotlight to hit the same enemy deals 75% less Final Damage.
Cooldown: 120 sec

Active Trinity Fusion
Master Level 25
Description Summon spotlights and dazzle your enemies with your stage presence. This skill can be activated while Trinity is in use as well.
Cannot be pushed back when casting, and any damage taken will be reduced. Trinity Fusion is unaffected by attack reflection, and upon a successful hit, will apply any stacked damage increase and/or Ignore Enemy DEF.
When Action Customization is enabled, use Trinity with the Down key to activate.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization On/Off

Active Grand Finale
Master Level 30
Description Drop an entire concert on the spot! Fans release colorful balloons to celebrate. After the concert ends, the Soul Seeker temporarily changes to Cheering Balloons.
Temporarily applies the effects of Affinity Heart. Cheering Balloons are created only when Soul Seeker Expert is active, and target the boss with the highest Max HP first. Unaffected by attack reflection.

Lv. 10 - Ignore Defense: +20%
Lv. 20 - Boss Damage: +20%
Lv. 30 - Ignore Defense: +30%, Boss Damage: +30%
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000, Invincible during casting, applies Affinity effect for 30 sec
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 346%, Number of Attacks: 9, Sound Waves: 12. Afterward, Damage: 355%, Number of Attacks: 14, Cannon Roars: 38
25 Cheering Balloons at the finale target enemies.
Afterwards, Soul Seekers change to Cheering Balloons for 30 sec.
Cheering Balloons - Cheering Balloons deal 345% damage, while Cheering Balloons created while the buff is active deal 441% damage and attack 7 times, with the same chance to respawn upon hit as Soul Seekers. Each subsequent Cheering Balloon created while the buff is active that hits the same enemy deals 43% less Final Damage.
Additional Cheering Balloons: 10, Cheering Balloons that fly in the finale only have Pretty Exaltation's increased respawn chance, and Soul Seekers that become Cheering Balloons have all of Pretty Exaltation's effects. Cooldown: 360 sec.
30 MP Cost: 1000, Invincible during casting, applies Affinity effect for 30 sec
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 694%, Number of Attacks: 9, Sound Waves: 12. Afterward, Damage: 703%, Number of Attacks: 14, Cannon Roars: 38
25 Cheering Balloons at the finale target enemies.
Afterwards, Soul Seekers change to Cheering Balloons for 30 sec.
Cheering Balloons - Cheering Balloons deal 490% damage, while Cheering Balloons created while the buff is active deal 673% damage and attack 7 times, with the same chance to respawn upon hit as Soul Seekers. Each subsequent Cheering Balloon created while the buff is active that hits the same enemy deals 43% less Final Damage.
Additional Cheering Balloons: 10, Cheering Balloons that fly in the finale only have Pretty Exaltation's increased respawn chance, and Soul Seekers that become Cheering Balloons have all of Pretty Exaltation's effects. Cooldown: 360 sec.

Each subsequent Cheering Balloon created while the buff is active that hits the same enemy deals 43% less Final Damage.
Additional Cheering Balloons: 10, Cheering Balloons that fly in the finale only have Pretty Exaltation's increased respawn chance, and Soul Seekers that become Cheering Balloons have all of Pretty Exaltation's effects. Cooldown: 360 sec.

Active HEXA Soul Seeker Expert
Master Level 30
Description Grants a chance to automatically create a Soul Seeker upon landing attacking skills (excludes Soul Buster, Soul Seeker, and Superstar Spotlight). Soul Seeker prioritizes the boss with the highest Max HP if within range.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Required Skill: Soul Seeker Expert Lv. 10
Level 1 36% chance to create Soul Seeker when using Angelic Buster skills (excluding Soul Buster, Soul Seeker, and Superstar Spotlight)
Celestial Roar and Trinity Creation Chance: +25%
Automatically created Soul Seekers deal 75% damage of directly created Soul Seekers

Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
